get_ge_leader_target = {
	random_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			has_leader_flag = $flag$
		}
		save_event_target_as = ge_leader
	}
}

generate_sgt_site_on_game_start = {
	##scope = country
	random_planet_within_border = {
		weights = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_capital = yes
			}
		}
		solar_system = {
			closest_system = {
				min_steps = 0
				max_steps = 17
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_star_flag = ge_suigintou_site_counted
					}
					has_owner = no
					has_access_fleet = root
					roz_sgt_site_planet_select_condition = yes
				}
				this = {
					set_star_flag = ge_suigintou_site_star_flag
				}
				set_timed_star_flag = {
					flag = ge_suigintou_site_counted
					days = 1
				}
				random_system_planet = {
					limit = {
						roz_sgt_site_planet_select_condition = yes
					}
					set_name = "NAME_ge_sgt_site_planet"
					change_pc = pc_black_hole
					set_planet_size = 1
					clear_deposits = yes
					set_planet_flag = ge_planet_flag_sgt@root
					create_archaeological_site = ge_sgt_site
					root = {
						set_country_flag = ge_sgt_site_owner_flag_for_multiplayer
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

create_ge_suigintou_scientist = {
	###水银灯-做科学家
	optimize_memory
	set_country_flag = ge_suigintou_scientist_active
	every_owned_leader = {#取当前水银灯为临时target
		limit = {
			has_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
		}
		save_event_target_as = ge_leader_suigintou_target_temp 
	}
	#缓存国家目标领袖更新替换,当前水银灯为舰队司令，要转科学家,先kill了再说
	event_target:ge_suigintou_admiral_inactive_temp@root = { #令临时存储国家的舰队司令水银灯消失
		kill_leader = {
			show_notification = no
		}
	}
	clone_leader = {
		#替换，event_target:ge_suigintou_country是水银灯的缓存国家
		#target = event_target:ge_leader_suigintou_global_target #这个global target是玩家的水银灯
		target = event_target:ge_leader_suigintou_target_temp  #刚刚存的target
		effect = {
			save_global_event_target_as = ge_suigintou_admiral_inactive_temp@root
			unassign_leader = this
			set_owner = event_target:ge_suigintou_country@root #存到临时存储国家
			freeze_leader_age = yes
			roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
				who_jp = Suigintou
				who_sc = shuiyindeng
			}
		}
	}
	every_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp_scientist
				has_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp
				has_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
				is_variable_set = ge_leader_affection
			}
		}
		unassign_leader = this
		kill_leader = {
			show_notification = no
		}
	}
	owner = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				event_target:ge_suigintou_country@root = {
					any_owned_leader = {
						leader_class = scientist
						has_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp_scientist
					}
				}
			}
			roz_suigintou_clone_scientist_from_cache_country = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { }
			create_leader = {
				class = scientist
				name = "NAME_Suigintou"
				skill = 1
				gender = female
				species = owner_main_species
				immortal = yes
				event_leader = yes
				set_age = 17
				traits = { }
				skip_background_generation = yes
				custom_catch_phrase = suigintou_sci_catch_phrase
				custom_description = suigintou_backstory
				effect = {
					add_skill_without_trait_selection = 1
					remove_all_traits = yes
					#change_leader_portrait = ge_suigintou_6
					set_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value = owner.ge_leader_aft_sgt
					}
				}
			}
			last_created_leader = {
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_meimei_scientist
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_N_field_scientist
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp_scientist
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_surveyor }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_midas_touch }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_knowledge_for_the_masses }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_great_researcher }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_truth_seeker }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_brilliant_shipwright }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_frontier_adventurer }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_xeno_cataloger }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_knowledge_for_the_masses }
				}
				freeze_leader_age = yes
			}
		}
		
	}
	roz_suigintou_initialize_scientist = yes
	remove_country_flag = ge_suigintou_admiral_active
}



create_ge_suigintou_admiral = {
	###水银灯-做舰队司令
	optimize_memory
	set_country_flag = ge_suigintou_admiral_active
	#缓存国家目标领袖更新替换
	event_target:ge_suigintou_scientist_inactive_temp@root = { #科学家
		kill_leader = {
			show_notification = no
		}
	}
	clone_leader = { #替换
		target = event_target:ge_leader_suigintou_global_target@root #直接用global target了，懒得存个新的
		effect = {
			save_global_event_target_as = ge_suigintou_scientist_inactive_temp@root
			unassign_leader = this
			set_owner = event_target:ge_suigintou_country@root
			freeze_leader_age = yes
			roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
				who_jp = Suigintou
				who_sc = shuiyindeng
			}
		}
	}
	every_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp_scientist
				has_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp
				has_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
				is_variable_set = ge_leader_affection
			}
		}
		unassign_leader = this
		kill_leader = {
			show_notification = no
		}
	}
	owner = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				event_target:ge_suigintou_country@root = {
					any_owned_leader = {
						leader_class = commander
						has_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp			
					}
				}
			}
			roz_suigintou_clone_admiral_from_cache_country = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { }
			create_leader = {
				class = commander
				species = owner_main_species
				gender = female
				name = "NAME_Suigintou"
				skill = 2
				set_age = 17
				event_leader = yes
				traits = { }
				skip_background_generation = yes
				custom_catch_phrase = suigintou_adm_catch_phrase
				custom_description = suigintou_backstory
				effect = {
					add_skill_without_trait_selection = 1
					remove_all_traits = yes
					#change_leader_portrait = ge_suigintou_6
					set_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value = owner.ge_leader_aft_sgt
					}
					roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
						who_jp = Suigintou
						who_sc = shuiyindeng
					}
				}
			}
			last_created_leader = {
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_Blackwinged_Dragon
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_azoth
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_N_field
				random_list = {
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_armorer }
					2 = { add_trait = leader_trait_military_overseer }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_master_gunner }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_destiny_engineer }
					2 = { add_trait = leader_trait_guerilla_tactics }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_survivalist }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_maven_of_war }
					1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_peacekeeper }
				}
				freeze_leader_age = yes
			}
		}
	}
	roz_suigintou_initialize_admiral = yes
	remove_country_flag = ge_suigintou_scientist_active
}

###clone suigintou
roz_suigintou_clone_scientist_from_cache_country = {
	clone_leader = {#从临时国家取科学家水银灯到玩家国家
		target = event_target:ge_suigintou_scientist_inactive_temp@root
		custom_catch_phrase = suigintou_sci_catch_phrase
		custom_description = suigintou_backstory
		effect = {
			freeze_leader_age = yes
			roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
				who_jp = Suigintou
				who_sc = shuiyindeng
			}
			set_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
			set_owner = event_target:ge_suigintou_owner@root
		}
	}
}

roz_suigintou_clone_admiral_from_cache_country = {
	clone_leader = {
		target = event_target:ge_suigintou_admiral_inactive_temp@root
		custom_catch_phrase = suigintou_sci_catch_phrase
		custom_description = suigintou_backstory
		effect = {
			#set_name = "NAME_Suigintou"
			freeze_leader_age = yes
			roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
				who_jp = Suigintou
				who_sc = shuiyindeng
			}
			set_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
			set_owner = event_target:ge_suigintou_owner@root
		}
	}
}

###initialize
roz_suigintou_initialize_scientist = {
	last_created_leader = {
		set_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
		set_leader_flag = legendary_leader
		set_leader_flag = immune_to_negative_traits
		#set_leader_flag = has_gained_level_trait
		roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
			who_jp = Suigintou
			who_sc = shuiyindeng
		}
		save_global_event_target_as = ge_leader_suigintou_global_target@root
		set_variable = {
			which = ge_leader_affection
			value = root.ge_leader_aft_sgt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 90 } }
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_scientist_a_love
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 60 } }
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_scientist_a_like
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 30 } }
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_scientist_a_friendly
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value < 30 } }
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_scientist_a_strangeness
		}
		freeze_leader_age = yes
	}
	#roz_leader_change_skin_set_flag_effect = {
	#	who = sgt
	#	portrait = ge_suigintou
	#	flag = ge_sgt_portrait_change
	#	leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
	#	portrait_key = ge_suigintou_6
	#}
	roz_leader_change_skin_reset_suigintou_effect = yes
}

roz_suigintou_initialize_admiral = {
	last_created_leader = {
		set_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
		set_leader_flag = legendary_leader
		set_leader_flag = immune_to_negative_traits
		save_global_event_target_as = ge_leader_suigintou_global_target@root
		set_variable = {
			which = ge_leader_affection
			value = root.ge_leader_aft_sgt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 90 } }
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_admiral_a_love
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 60 } }
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_admiral_a_like
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 30 } }
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_admiral_a_friendly
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value < 30 } }
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_admiral_a_strangeness
		}
		freeze_leader_age = yes
	}
	#roz_leader_change_skin_set_flag_effect = {
	#	who = sgt
	#	portrait = ge_suigintou
	#	flag = ge_sgt_portrait_change
	#	leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
	#	portrait_key = ge_suigintou_6
	#}
	roz_leader_change_skin_reset_suigintou_effect = yes
}

##############
###检测水银灯是否重复
roz_leader_suigintou_counting_check = {
	#Scope = player country
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ge_leader_suigintou_get
			NOR = {	#由于存在相当多遍历，因此该封装中期后或领袖太多时将不再检测
				mid_game_years_passed > 0
				num_owned_leaders >= 24
			}
		}
		every_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp_scientist
					has_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp
					has_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
					is_variable_set = ge_leader_affection
				}
				NOT = {
					has_leader_flag = roz_suigintou_checking_flag
				}
			}
			set_leader_flag = roz_suigintou_checking_flag
			Root = {
				change_variable = {
					which = roz_suigintou_counting_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = roz_suigintou_counting_var
					value > 1
				}
			}
			while = {
				count = roz_suigintou_counting_var
				random_owned_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_leader_flag = roz_suigintou_checking_flag
					}
					kill_leader = {
						show_notification = no
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable = roz_suigintou_counting_var
			every_owned_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = roz_suigintou_checking_flag
				}
				remove_leader_flag = roz_suigintou_checking_flag
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = roz_suigintou_counting_var
					value <= 1
				}
			}
			clear_variable = roz_suigintou_counting_var
			every_owned_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = roz_suigintou_checking_flag
				}
				remove_leader_flag = roz_suigintou_checking_flag
			}
		}
	}
}















#####leader suigintou backup (from cache country)
roz_suigintou_scientist_backup = {
	#scientist
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ge_suigintou_scientist_active
			event_target:ge_leader_suigintou_global_target@root = {
				leader_class = scientist
			}
		}
		#缓存国家目标领袖更新替换
		event_target:ge_suigintou_scientist_inactive_temp@root = {
			kill_leader = {
				show_notification = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			clone_leader = { #替换
				target = event_target:ge_leader_suigintou_global_target@root
				custom_catch_phrase = suigintou_sci_catch_phrase
				custom_description = suigintou_backstory
				effect = {
					save_global_event_target_as = ge_suigintou_scientist_inactive_temp@root
					unassign_leader = this
					set_owner = event_target:ge_suigintou_country@root
					freeze_leader_age = yes
					roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
						who_jp = Suigintou
						who_sc = shuiyindeng
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

roz_suigintou_admiral_backup = {
	#admiral
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ge_suigintou_admiral_active
			event_target:ge_leader_suigintou_global_target@root = {
				leader_class = commander
			}
		}
		#缓存国家目标领袖更新替换
		event_target:ge_suigintou_admiral_inactive_temp@root = { #令临时存储国家的舰队司令水银灯消失
			kill_leader = {
				show_notification = no
			}
		}
		clone_leader = {
			target = event_target:ge_leader_suigintou_global_target@root

				roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
					who_jp = Suigintou
					who_sc = shuiyindeng
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


###revive suigintou for cache country
roz_suigintou_revive_reset_scientist = {
	event_target:ge_suigintou_country@root = {
		create_leader = {
			class = scientist
			name = "NAME_Suigintou"
			skill = 1
			gender = female
			species = owner_main_species
			immortal = yes
			event_leader = yes
			set_age = 17
			traits = { }
			skip_background_generation = yes
			custom_catch_phrase = suigintou_sci_catch_phrase
			custom_description = suigintou_backstory
			effect = {
				add_skill_without_trait_selection = 1
				remove_all_traits = yes
				#change_leader_portrait = ge_suigintou_6
				#set_variable = {
				#	which = ge_leader_affection
				#	value = owner.ge_leader_aft_sgt
				#}
			}
		}
		last_created_leader = {
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_meimei_scientist
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_N_field_scientist
			add_trait = leader_trait_ge_mercury_lamp_scientist
			random_list = {
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_surveyor }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_midas_touch }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_knowledge_for_the_masses }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_great_researcher }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_truth_seeker }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_brilliant_shipwright }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_frontier_adventurer }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_xeno_cataloger }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_knowledge_for_the_masses }
			}
			freeze_leader_age = yes
		}
		last_created_leader = {
			set_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
			set_leader_flag = legendary_leader
			set_leader_flag = immune_to_negative_traits
			roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
				who_jp = Suigintou
				who_sc = shuiyindeng
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = ge_leader_affection
				value = root.ge_leader_aft_sgt
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 90 } }
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_scientist_a_love
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 60 } }
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_scientist_a_like
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 30 } }
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_scientist_a_friendly
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value < 30 } }
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_scientist_a_strangeness
			}
			freeze_leader_age = yes
		}
		roz_leader_change_skin_set_flag_effect = {
			who = sgt
			portrait = ge_suigintou
			flag = ge_sgt_portrait_change
			leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
			portrait_key = ge_suigintou_6
		}
		save_global_event_target_as = ge_suigintou_scientist_inactive_temp@root
	}
}

				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_survivalist }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_maven_of_war }
				1 = { add_trait = leader_trait_peacekeeper }
			}
			freeze_leader_age = yes
		}
		last_created_leader = {
			set_leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
			set_leader_flag = legendary_leader
			set_leader_flag = immune_to_negative_traits
			set_variable = {
				which = ge_leader_affection
				value = root.ge_leader_aft_sgt
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 90 } }
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_admiral_a_love
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 60 } }
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_admiral_a_like
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value >= 30 } }
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_admiral_a_friendly
			}
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = ge_leader_affection value < 30 } }
				add_trait = leader_trait_ge_admiral_a_strangeness
			}
			freeze_leader_age = yes
		}
		roz_leader_change_skin_set_flag_effect = {
			who = sgt
			portrait = ge_suigintou
			flag = ge_sgt_portrait_change
			leader_flag = ge_suigintou_flag
			portrait_key = ge_suigintou_6
		}
		save_global_event_target_as = ge_suigintou_admiral_inactive_temp@root
	}
}

ge_leader_affection = {

		which = ge_leader_affection
		value = 0
	}
}

# 
ge_add_random_var = {
	optimize_memory
	random_list = {
		60 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value <= 30
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value <= 60
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 0.75
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value <= 90
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value < 100
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value >= 100
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
		20 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value <= 30
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value <= 60
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value <= 90
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value < 100
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ge_leader_affection
						value >= 100
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_custom_variable
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
		20 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = ge_custom_variable
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

ge_add_aft_admiral_wander = {
	optimize_memory
	ge_add_random_var = yes
	divide_variable = {
		which = ge_custom_variable
		value = 15
	}
	change_variable = {
		which = ge_leader_affection
		value = ge_custom_variable
	}
	clear_variable = ge_custom_variable
}

	}

		value = ge_custom_variable
	}
	clear_variable = ge_custom_variable
}

ge_add_aft_scientist_on_research = {
	optimize_memory
	#随机数，0.5-2-0
	ge_add_random_var = yes
	###与科研三产挂钩，增加变量
	root = {
		export_resource_income_to_variable = {
			resource = physics_research
			variable = roz_aft_temp_var
		}
		export_resource_income_to_variable = {
			resource = society_research
			variable = roz_aft_temp_var
		}
		export_resource_income_to_variable = {
			resource = engineering_research
			variable = roz_aft_temp_var
		}
		#divide_variable = {
		#	which = roz_aft_temp_var
		#	value = 3
		#}
		divide_variable = {
			which = roz_aft_temp_var
			value = 300
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = roz_aft_temp_var
		value = root.roz_aft_temp_var
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = roz_aft_temp_var
				value <= 0
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = ge_custom_variable
			value = 0
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = roz_aft_temp_var
				value > 0
			}
			check_variable = {
				which = roz_aft_temp_var
				value < 2.5
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = ge_custom_variable
			value = roz_aft_temp_var
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = roz_aft_temp_var
				value >= 2.5
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = ge_custom_variable
			value = 2.5
		}
	}
	###
	divide_variable = {
		which = ge_custom_variable
		value = 20
	}
	change_variable = {
		which = ge_leader_affection
		value = ge_custom_variable
		#value = 1
	}
	clear_variable = ge_custom_variable
	clear_variable =roz_aft_temp_var
	root = {
		clear_variable = roz_aft_temp_var
	}
}

roz_add_aft_govern_planet = { #蔷薇少女在星球上任职时,增加好感度
	if = {
		limit = { 
			event_target:ge_leader_suigintou_global_target@root = {
				planet = {
					exists = this
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			 event_target:ge_leader_suigintou_global_target@root = {
				change_variable = {
					which = ge_leader_affection
					value = 0.03
				}
			 }
		}
	}
}

################################fleet
create_ge_defense_ship = {
	optimize_memory
	while = {
		count = 6
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_technology = tech_corvettes
				}
			}
			create_ship = {
				name = random
				design = "NAME_ge_anti-invasion_corvette"
				graphical_culture = owner
			}
		}
	}
	while = {
		count = 4
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_technology = tech_destroyers
				}
			}
			create_ship = {
				name = random
				design = "NAME_ge_anti-invasion_destroyer"
				graphical_culture = owner
			}
		}
	}
	while = {
		count = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_technology = tech_battleships
				}
			}
			create_ship = {
				name = random
				design = "NAME_ge_anti-invasion_battleship"
				graphical_culture = owner
			}
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	}
}

create_ge_kirakishou_hostile_ship = {
	optimize_memory
	#鸡精建国，刷船
	create_species = {
		name = random
		class = random_non_machine
		portrait = random
		traits = {
			ideal_planet_class = pc_habitat
			trait = random_traits
		}
		#homeworld = this
	}
	create_country = {
		name = "NAME_kirakishou_hostile_country"
		type = enclave
		authority = "auth_oligarchic"
		civics = {
			civic = civic_ancient_preservers
		}
		origin = "origin_default"
		species = last_created_species
		flag = {
			icon = {
				category = "enclaves"
				file = "enclaves_flag_curator.dds"
			}
			background = {
				category = "backgrounds"
				file = "vertical.dds"
			}
			colors = {
				"white"
				"red"
				"null"
				"null"
			}
		}
		ethos = {
			ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
			ethic = ethic_pacifist
		}
		ignore_initial_colony_error = yes
	}
	last_created_country = {
		set_country_flag = kirakishou_hostile_country
		set_graphical_culture = mammalian_01
		save_global_event_target_as = kirakishou_hostile_country@root
		set_hostile = root
		establish_communications_no_message = root
		create_fleet = {
			name = "NAME_ge_kirakishou_hostile_fleet"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
				is_boss = yes
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = prev
				create_ship = {
					name = "NAME_ge_kirakishou_hostile_fleet"
					design = "NAME_ge_kirakishou_hostile_ship"
					graphical_culture = prev
					effect = {
						#set_timed_ship_flag = {
						#	flag = invincible
						#	days = 10
						#}
					}
				}
				set_location = {
					target = prevprev
					angle = random
					distance = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_flag = roz_krks_dl_normal_flag
						}
					}
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = roz_krks_bf_stage1_HK_buff
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_flag = roz_krks_dl_early_flag
						}
					}
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = roz_krks_bf_stage1_HK_buff
						mult = 0.0005
					}
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = kirakishou_Avatar_fleet@root
				set_fleet_flag = kirakishou_Avatar_fleet_flag
				set_fleet_flag = kirakishou_hostile_fleet_flag
				prev = {
					#set_custom_capital_location = event_target:kirakishou_Avatar
				}
			}
		}

		create_fleet = {
			name = "NAME_roz_krks_zakko"
			settings = {
				spawn_debris = no
				is_boss = no
			}
			effect = {
				set_owner = last_created_country
				if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_flag = roz_krks_dl_normal_flag
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = 3
						create_ship = {
							name = "NAME_Corrupted_Avatar"
							design = "NAME_Corrupted_Avatar"
							effect = {
								#set_timed_ship_flag = { #如果你开了mist
								#	flag = invincible
								#	days = 3
								#}
							}
						}
						set_location = event_target:ge_site_sgt_target
						set_fleet_stance = aggressive
						set_aggro_range_measure_from = return_point
						set_aggro_range = 300

						add_modifier = {
							modifier = roz_krks_bf_stage1_HK_buff
						}
					}
				}

				else_if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_flag = roz_krks_dl_early_flag
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}

	}
}

							#	days = 3
							#}
						}
					}
					set_location = event_target:ge_site_sgt_target
					set_fleet_stance = aggressive
					set_aggro_range_measure_from = return_point
					set_aggro_range = 300

					add_modifier = {
						modifier = roz_krks_bf_stage1_HK_buff
					}
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = {
					root = {
						has_country_flag = roz_krks_dl_early_flag
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}

}

				name = "NAME_ge_kirakishou_hostile_fleet"

				}
			}

				}
			}

			set_fleet_flag = kirakishou_everything_fleet_flag
			set_fleet_flag = kirakishou_hostile_fleet_flag

	}

		name = "NAME_roz_krks_zakko"
		settings = {
			spawn_debris = no
			is_boss = no
		}

				limit = {

					}
				}

					count = 6

						name = "NAME_Corrupted_Avatar"

							#set_timed_ship_flag = { #如果你开了mist

							#}

					}
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = {
					root = {
						has_country_flag = roz_krks_dl_early_flag
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}

	optimize_memory
	every_owned_leader = {
		limit = {

		}

		exile_leader_as = this
	}
	every_owned_fleet = {
		limit = {
			is_ship_size = ge_black_dragon
		}
		solar_system = {
			create_ambient_object = {
				type = "star_explosion"
				duration = 5
				#play_animation_once = yes
				entity_scale_to_size = no
				use_3d_location = yes
				entity_offset = { min = 0 max = 0 }
				entity_offset_angle = { min = 0 max = 0 }
				entity_offset_height = { min = 0 max = 0 }
				scale = 4
				location = this
			}
			create_ambient_object = {
				type = nebula_1
				duration = 30
				#play_animation_once = yes
				entity_scale_to_size = no
				use_3d_location = yes
				entity_offset = { min = 0 max = 0 }
				entity_offset_angle = { min = 0 max = 0 }
				entity_offset_height = { min = 0 max = 0 }
				scale = 2
				location = this
			}
		}

		destroy_fleet = this
	}
	#清理全局目标,以及flag
	event_target:kirakishou_hostile_country@root = {
		destroy_country = yes
	}
	clear_global_event_target = kirakishou_hostile_country
	clear_global_event_target = kirakishou_Avatar_fleet

	remove_country_flag = roz_bf_stage3_flag

		}

	}
	every_situation = { limit = { is_situation_type = kirakishou_battle_field_situation }destroy_situation = this }

		limit = {
			has_country_flag = roz_krks_dl_normal_flag
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = ge_gravity_knowledge_plus
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = roz_krks_dl_early_flag
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = ge_gravity_knowledge
		}
	}
	capital_scope = {
		switch = {
			trigger = has_modifier
			ge_kirakishou_invasion_lv1 = {

			}

				remove_modifier = ge_kirakishou_invasion_lv3

ge_ship_modifier_intercepting = {#
	optimize_memory
	#set_update_modifiers_batch = begin
	if = {
		limit = {
			#NOT = {
			#	has_ship_flag = roz_ship_buff_cooldown_flag
			#}
			check_modifier_value = {
				modifier = $modifier$
				value >= -1
			}
		}
		export_modifier_to_variable = {
			modifier = $modifier$
			variable = $modifier$_value_ge
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = $modifier$_value_ge
			value = $subtract|0$
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = $modifier$_value_ge
			value = $change|0$
		}
		divide_variable = {
			which = $modifier$_value_ge
			value = $divide|1$
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = $modifier$_value_ge
			value = $multiply|1$
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = ge_basic_$modifier$
			multiplier = $modifier$_value_ge
			days = $DAYS$
		}
		clear_variable = $modifier$_value_ge
		###
		#owner = {
		#	change_variable = {
		#		which = $modifier$_value_ge
		#		value = root.$modifier$_value_ge
		#	}
		#}
		###
		#
		###buff累计计数
	}
	#else_if = {
	#	limit = {
	#		NOT = {
	#			has_ship_flag = roz_ship_buff_cooldown_flag
	#		}
	#		check_modifier_value = {
	#			modifier = $modifier$
	#			value < 0
	#		}
	#		check_modifier_value = {
	#			modifier = $modifier$
	#			value > $PARA1$
	#		}
	#	}
	#	export_modifier_to_variable = {
	#		modifier = $modifier$
	#		variable = $modifier$_value_ge
	#	}
	#	subtract_variable = {
	#		which = $modifier$_value_ge
	#		value = 0
	#	}
	#	change_variable = {
	#		which = $modifier$_value_ge
	#		value = 0
	#	}
	#	divide_variable = {
	#		which = $modifier$_value_ge
	#		value = 1
	#	}
	#	multiply_variable = {
	#		which = $modifier$_value_ge
	#		value = 1
	#	}
	#	add_modifier = {
	#		modifier = ge_basic_$modifier$
	#		multiplier = $modifier$_value_ge
	#		days = $DAYS$
	#	}
	#	clear_variable = $modifier$_value_ge
	#}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_modifier_value = {
				modifier = $modifier$
				value < -1
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = ge_basic_$modifier$
			multiplier = 15
			days = $DAYS$
		}
	}
	#set_update_modifiers_batch = end
	#set_timed_ship_flag = { flag = roz_ship_buff_cooldown_flag days = 2 }
}



######################################
ge_generater_effect = {
	optimize_memory
	
	every_owned_fleet = {
		limit = { 
			any_owned_ship = {
				has_component = ge_shippart_hyper_generator
				is_ship_size = $ship_size$				
			}
		}
		
		export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
			trigger = num_ships
			variable = ge_fleet_generatorship_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				any_owned_ship = {
					NOR = {
						has_component_ZERO_POINT_REACTOR = yes
					}
					NOR = {
						has_component_DARK_MATTER_REACTOR = yes
					}
					OR = {
						has_component_GE_REACTOR = yes
					}
				}
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ge_fleet_generatorship_var
				value = 10
			}
		}
		root = {
			change_variable = {
				which = ge_country_generatorship_var
				value = prev.ge_fleet_generatorship_var
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ge_country_generatorship_var
				value = $cash_mult$
			}
			add_resource = {
				energy = 0.1
				mult = ge_country_generatorship_var
			}
		}
		clear_variable = ge_fleet_generatorship_var
	}
}

	give_technology = { tech = tech_fe_administration_2 }

	give_technology = { tech = tech_fe_assembly_2 }

	give_technology = { tech = tech_fe_clinic_2 }

	give_technology = { tech = tech_fe_market_2 }

	give_technology = { tech = tech_fe_silo_2 }

	give_technology = { tech = tech_fe_entertainment_2 }

	give_technology = { tech = tech_fe_lab_2 }

	give_technology = { tech = tech_fe_mine_2 }


	random_system_planet = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_planet_class = pc_gray_goo
				is_planet_class = pc_barren
				is_planet_class = pc_barren_cold
			}
			#always = no
		}
		set_name = NAME_roz_lgate
		change_pc = pc_city
		change_planet_size = 25
		clear_deposits = yes
		clear_blockers = yes
		set_owner = root
		#set_capital = yes
		while = {
			count = 160
			create_pop = {
				species = root
				ethos = root
			}
		}
		while = {
			count = 3
			add_district = district_arcology_civilian_industry
		}
		while = {
			count = 5
			add_district = district_arcology_arms_industry
		}
		while = {
			count = 5
			add_district = district_arcology_leisure
		}
		while = {
			count = 5
			add_district = district_arcology_housing
		}
		while = {
			count = 2
			limit = {
				Root = {
					NOR = {
						has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
						has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					}
				}
			}
			add_district = district_arcology_administrative
		}

		while = {
			count = 3
			limit = {
				Root = {
					OR = {
						has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
						has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					}
				}
			}
			add_district = district_arcology_religious
		}
		add_deposit = d_meals_in_pods
		add_deposit = d_prisoner_intergration
		add_deposit = d_ancient_particle_accelerator
		add_deposit = d_alien_sanctuary
		add_deposit = d_betharian_deposit
		add_building = building_roz_ancient_palace
		add_building = building_roz_fe_stronghold
		add_building = building_roz_fe_dome
		add_building = building_roz_master_archive
		add_building = building_roz_nano_forge
		add_building =  building_roz_class_5_singularity
		add_building = building_roz_dimensional_fabricator
		add_building = building_roz_nourishment_center
		add_building = building_roz_affluence_center
		add_building = building_roz_fe_administration_2
		add_building = building_roz_fe_clinic_2
		add_building = building_roz_fe_market_2
		add_building = building_roz_fe_silo_2
		add_building = building_roz_fe_entertainment_2
		add_building = building_roz_fe_lab_2
		add_building = building_roz_fe_mine_2

	}
}

roz_site_inline_math = {
	add_monthly_resource_mult = {
		resource = $RESOURCE$
		value = $COUNT|1$
		min = @\[$COUNT|1$*5]
		max = 50000
	}
}

roz_teaparty_loop_random = { #root = player country
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_101 }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_101 value = 0 }

	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_101 } }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_101 value = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_102 }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_102 value = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_102 } }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_102 value = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_103 }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_103 value = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_103 } }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_103 value = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_104 }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_104 value = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_104 } }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_104 value = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_105 }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_105 value = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_105 } }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_105 value = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_106 }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_106 value = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_106 } }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_106 value = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_107 }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_107 value = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_107 } }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_107 value = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_108 }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_108 value = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_108 } }
		set_variable = { which = roz_teaparty_108 value = 1 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_101
			has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_102
			has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_103
			has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_104
			has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_105
			has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_106
			has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_107
			has_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_108
		}
		remove_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_101
		remove_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_102
		remove_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_103
		remove_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_104
		remove_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_105
		remove_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_106
		remove_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_107
		remove_country_flag = roz_teaparty_evt_108
	}
	random_list = {
		1 = { country_event = { id = roz_teaparty_evt.101 } }
		1 = { country_event = { id = roz_teaparty_evt.102 } }
		1 = { country_event = { id = roz_teaparty_evt.103 } }
		1 = { country_event = { id = roz_teaparty_evt.104 } }
		1 = { country_event = { id = roz_teaparty_evt.105 } }
		1 = { country_event = { id = roz_teaparty_evt.106 } }
		1 = { country_event = { id = roz_teaparty_evt.107 } }
		1 = { country_event = { id = roz_teaparty_evt.108 } }
	}
}

	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_3
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_4
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_5
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_6
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_61
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_7
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_8
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_9
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_10
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_11

	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_14
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_15
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_20
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_21
	remove_country_flag = ge_$who$_portrait_change_$portrait$_22

}

roz_leader_change_skin_set_flag_effect = {
	roz_leader_change_skin_remove_all_flag_effect = {
		who = $who$
		portrait = $portrait$
	}
	set_country_flag = $flag$_$portrait_key$
	every_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			has_leader_flag = $leader_flag$
		}
		change_leader_portrait = $portrait_key$
	}
}

roz_leader_change_skin_flag_locate_effect = {
	roz_leader_change_skin_remove_all_flag_effect = {
		who = $who$
		portrait = $portrait$
	}
	set_country_flag = $flag$_$portrait_key$
	every_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			has_leader_flag = $leader_flag$
		}
		change_leader_portrait = $portrait_key$

	}
}

roz_leader_name_set_effect = {
	#root = player_country
	#this = leader
	if = {
		limit = {
			root = {
				has_country_flag = roz_leader_name_jp_flag
			}
		}
		set_name = NAME_$who_jp$
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			root = {
				has_country_flag = roz_leader_name_sc_flag
			}
		}
		set_name = NAME_$who_sc$
	}
}

chronos_storm_add = {
	set_star_flag = storm_system
	set_global_flag = cosmic_storm_has_occurred

	inline_script = {
		script = cosmic_storms/StormVisuals
		STORM_NAME = "chronos_storm"
	}
}

chronos_storm_remove = {
	remove_storm_visuals_effect = yes
	remove_star_flag = storm_system
	nexus_storm_apply_aftermath_modifier = yes
}
